<div class="content-general">
	<div class="zone-content">
		<div class="container">
			    		<h2 class="element-invisible">You are here</h2><div class="breadcrumb"><span class="inline odd first"><a href="/">Home</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline even"><a href="/about-us">About Us</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline odd last">Commitments &amp; Responsibility</span></div>												<h1 class="title">Commitments &amp; Responsibility</h1>
												<div class="tabs"></div>
						<div id="block-system-main" class="block block-system">

    
  <div class="content">
    <div class="node-full page-full">
  <div class="content">
    <div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"><p>We believe that a successful journey not only provides a memorable experience for our clients, but as tour operators we are responsible for respecting and conserving economic, environmental, and social-cultural balances.</p>
<p>Consequently We: </p>
<ul>
<li><strong>BELIEVE</strong> in sustainability. <strong>JUST ENJOY PERU</strong> is constantly strive to reduce our carbon footprint.</li>
<li>Understand and respect cultures by promoting and communicating their traditions, life styles and heritage to our travelers and to our team.</li>
<li>Support communities by involving and co-operating with local natives, utilizing local skills and products when possible.</li>
<li>Care for the environment by recycling, conserving landscapes, planting trees, and respecting protected areas</li>
<li>We encourage our staff and travelers to avoid “single-use plastic” and promote recycling.</li>
</ul>
<p>Our sustainability policy incorporates the Global Code of Ethics for Tourism to promote responsible and sustainable tourism in those destinations where we operate, minimizing actions that may generate a climatic change, aiming for the welfare of our employees, clients, partners, providers and the community.<br>
Our objectives are to set in place responsible practices that will have a minimal impact on the environments and communities in which we work while at the same time ensuring our clients enjoy a memorable trip.<br>
 </p>
</div></div></div>  </div>
</div>
 
  </div>
</div>

<div class="content-general">
	<div class="zone-content">
		<div class="container">
			    		<h2 class="element-invisible">You are here</h2><div class="breadcrumb"><span class="inline odd first"><a href="/">Home</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline even"><a href="/destinations">Destinations</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline odd"><a href="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/lima">Lima</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline even last">Pachacamac Archaeological Center</span></div>												<h1 class="title">Pachacamac Archaeological Center</h1>
												<div class="tabs"></div>
						<div id="block-system-main" class="block block-system">

    
  <div class="content">
    <div class="tours-full text-justify">
    <div class="field field-name-field-s field-type-image field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><div id="flexslider-1" class="flexslider optionset-default imagestyle-slider-tour">
  <ul class="slides"><li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/lima-pachacamac-slider-1.jpg?itok=mnJg113J" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/lima-pachacamac-slider-2.jpg?itok=S4qd6oXc" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/lima-pachacamac-slider-3.jpg?itok=DaHJgceU" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/lima-pachacamac-slider-4.jpg?itok=0I6nq3YP" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
</ul></div>
</div></div></div>    <div class="box">
        <div class="row">
            <div class="col-sm-9 description-tour"><div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"><p>We will pick you up from your Hotel and will have a bus ride along La Costa Verde, arriving and visiting the district of Chorrillos, the southern district in the Lima Bay, From there you will enjoy a stunning view of the whole bay of Lima. En route to Pachacamac complex, you will observe Pantanos de Villa, protected area of wetlands protecting bird fauna and preserving flora of the Peruvian costa. Following the Pan- American Highway to the south, we will be entering to the Lurin Valley where we will visit Pachacamac, the most important archaeological complex of the central coast located only 20km away from Lima. It has maintained several pyramids, temples and plazas, date from around 200 BC</p>
</div></div></div>            	 <div class="tour-acordion">
	               <div class="panel-group" id="accordion" role="tablist" aria-multiselectable="true">
		               		<div class="btns-itinerary"> 
        	                 
        	                <h2>Itinerary </h2>
				            	     <div class="content-buttons">
                                   <button type="button" class="btns-tour btn_expand" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion">unfold itinerary</button>
                            	   <button type="button" class="btns-tour btn_collapse" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion" data-target=".collapse.in">fold itinerary</button>  
                            	                         			                                 </div>
                        	</div>
                        	<div class="content-itinerary">
                    													<div class="panel panel-default">
            								<div class="panel-heading" role="tab" id="headingOne">
                								<h4 class="panel-title">
               									<button type="button" class="btn btn_acordion" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion" data-target="#collapse68"><span class="glyphicon glyphicon-triangle-bottom"></span><div class="field field-name-field-title-itinerary field-type-text field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>DAY 1</p>
</div></div></div></button>
	            								</h4>
            								</div>
           									<div id="collapse68" class="panel-collapse collapse">
                								<div class="panel-body">
                 									<div class="field field-name-field-description-itinerary field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>We will pick you up from your Hotel and will have a bus ride along La Costa Verde, arriving and visiting the district of Chorrillos, the southern district in the Lima Bay, From there you will enjoy a stunning view of the whole bay of Lima. En route to Pachacamac complex, you will observe Pantanos de Villa, protected area of wetlands protecting bird fauna and preserving flora of the Peruvian costa. Following the Pan- American Highway to the south, we will be entering to the Lurin Valley where we will visit Pachacamac, the most important archaeological complex of the central coast located only 20km away from Lima. It has maintained several pyramids, temples and plazas, date from around 200 BC. After walking and getting to know this outstanding complex next to the shoreline, we will have the return bus ride to your Hotel in Lima.ec</p>
</div></div></div>                								</div>
            								</div>
        								</div>
         														</div>

			    		<h2 class="element-invisible">You are here</h2><div class="breadcrumb"><span class="inline odd first"><a href="/">Home</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline even"><a href="/destinations">Destinations</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline odd"><a href="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/puno">Puno</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline even last">Taquile Uros Island</span></div>												<h1 class="title">Taquile Uros Island</h1>
												<div class="tabs"></div>
						<div id="block-system-main" class="block block-system">

    
  <div class="content">
    <div class="tours-full text-justify">
    <div class="field field-name-field-s field-type-image field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><div id="flexslider-1" class="flexslider optionset-default imagestyle-slider-tour">
  <ul class="slides"><li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/uros_1.jpg?itok=Pkz1hn2d" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/taquile1.jpg?itok=TnIEqycy" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/uros_2.jpg?itok=cQl7T3ay" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
</ul></div>
</div></div></div>    <div class="box">
        <div class="row">
            <div class="col-sm-9 description-tour"><div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"><p>This day we will visit the highest navigable lake in the World, The Lake Titicaca. We will be picked up from our hotel and transferred to our embarkation point, from where our boat will leave and take us to Taquile Island, stopping on the way at the Uros floating Islands.</p>
</div></div></div>            	 <div class="tour-acordion">
	               <div class="panel-group" id="accordion" role="tablist" aria-multiselectable="true">
		               		<div class="btns-itinerary"> 
        	                 
        	                <h2>Itinerary </h2>
				            	     <div class="content-buttons">
                                   <button type="button" class="btns-tour btn_expand" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion">unfold itinerary</button>
                            	   <button type="button" class="btns-tour btn_collapse" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion" data-target=".collapse.in">fold itinerary</button>  
                            	                         			                                 </div>
                        	</div>
                        	<div class="content-itinerary">
                    													<div class="panel panel-default">
            								<div class="panel-heading" role="tab" id="headingOne">
                								<h4 class="panel-title">
               									<button type="button" class="btn btn_acordion" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion" data-target="#collapse36"><span class="glyphicon glyphicon-triangle-bottom"></span><div class="field field-name-field-title-itinerary field-type-text field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>Taquile Uros Island</p>
</div></div></div></button>
	            								</h4>
            								</div>
           									<div id="collapse36" class="panel-collapse collapse">
                								<div class="panel-body">
                 									<div class="field field-name-field-description-itinerary field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>This day we will visit the highest navigable lake in the World, The Lake Titicaca. We will be picked up from our hotel and transferred to our embarkation point, from where our boat will leave and take us to Taquile Island, stopping on the way at the Uros floating Islands. Inheritors of an ancient culture, these Lake nomads rely on the lake resources to subsist, just as their ancestors did, while living on their floating islands made out of Totora Reed, a unique way of life. From here we will head to Taquile Island, and disembark on the local deck to visit the locals known as the Taquileños. These local peasants work under a communal economy, which has allowed them to subsist for centuries. On this isolated island the legend tell that this people escaped from the main land life, which was full of hardship, and developed a society based on mutual cooperation. Upon arrival to the Island we will climb the trail and steps up to the main plaza and walk around the village. Then we will visit a lodge managed by a local family where we will have a typical lunch. This tour will introduce you to the real way of life of Andean people. On the way back to Puno, we will visit the floating Island of Uros, known as one the most traditional towns of Peru. The small community of the Uros lives on floating islands along the Lake. These islands are constructed from a plant called “Junco” or “Totora”. In addition to the majesty of the landscape you will be able to see up close how these people live on these unique islands. Afternoon return to Puno and your hotel.</p>
</div></div></div>                								</div>
            								</div>
        								</div>
         														</div>

}
advagg_mod_1_check();</script><!-- end olark code -->  </div>
</div>

<div class="content-general">
	<div class="zone-content">
		<div class="container">
			    		<h2 class="element-invisible">You are here</h2><div class="breadcrumb"><span class="inline odd first"><a href="/">Home</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline even"><a href="/destinations">Destinations</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline odd"><a href="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/puno">Puno</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline even last">Aymara Route: Puno– Temple of Fertility - Chucuito– Aramu Muro - Juli – Pomata – Puno</span></div>												<h1 class="title">Aymara Route: Puno– Temple of Fertility - Chucuito– Aramu Muro - Juli – Pomata – Puno</h1>
												<div class="tabs"></div>
						<div id="block-system-main" class="block block-system">

    
  <div class="content">
    <div class="tours-full text-justify">
    <div class="field field-name-field-s field-type-image field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><div id="flexslider-1" class="flexslider optionset-default imagestyle-slider-tour">
  <ul class="slides"><li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/chucuito4.jpg?itok=gvrjqkX7" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/chucuito2.jpg?itok=XVI4_KWp" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/chucuito3.jpg?itok=xCXntEZy" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/chucuito.jpg?itok=891vjCUE" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
</ul></div>
</div></div></div>    <div class="box">
        <div class="row">
            <div class="col-sm-9 description-tour"><div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"><p>We visited the Totora´s Museum, an artistic demonstration of the importance of the totora in daily living in the altiplano</p>
</div></div></div>            	 <div class="tour-acordion">
	               <div class="panel-group" id="accordion" role="tablist" aria-multiselectable="true">
		               		<div class="btns-itinerary"> 
        	                 
        	                <h2>Itinerary </h2>
				            	     <div class="content-buttons">
                                   <button type="button" class="btns-tour btn_expand" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion">unfold itinerary</button>
                            	   <button type="button" class="btns-tour btn_collapse" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion" data-target=".collapse.in">fold itinerary</button>  
                            	                         			                                 </div>
                        	</div>
                        	<div class="content-itinerary">
                    													<div class="panel panel-default">
            								<div class="panel-heading" role="tab" id="headingOne">
                								<h4 class="panel-title">
               									<button type="button" class="btn btn_acordion" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion" data-target="#collapse34"><span class="glyphicon glyphicon-triangle-bottom"></span><div class="field field-name-field-title-itinerary field-type-text field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>DAY 1</p>
</div></div></div></button>
	            								</h4>
            								</div>
           									<div id="collapse34" class="panel-collapse collapse">
                								<div class="panel-body">
                 									<div class="field field-name-field-description-itinerary field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>07.00 Departure from the Hotel to the South of Puno, we go to the road that connects Puno and Bolivia, (the border) Aymara sector.<br>
07.15 We visited the Totora´s Museum, an artistic demonstration of the importance of the totora in daily living in the altiplano<br>
08.45 We visited Aramu Muro. At Km 75 we will arrive at Hayu Marca also known as Aramu Muru, the gateway to the four dimensions. People wait for the arrival of the golden solar disk that will enter through this door that will be the signal of well-being.<br>
10.00 We visited July, the Little Rome that has 4 colonial churches of the XVI century. July was the capital of the archdiocese and the most important place of the pre-Inca cultures of the altiplano<br>
11.30 We visited Pomata and its Colonial Church carved in stone<br>
12.30 We had lunch in a Tourist hotel and then we visited Chucuito and its temple of Fertility. We visited Inca Uyu, its colonial churches, the solar clock, the Cross of the Holy Inquisition and the trout fish farm.<br>
14.30 Return to Puno.<br>
16.00 Arrive to Puno and transfer to your hotel.</p>
</div></div></div>                								</div>
            								</div>

	<div class="zone-content">
		<div class="container">
			    		<h2 class="element-invisible">You are here</h2><div class="breadcrumb"><span class="inline odd first"><a href="/">Home</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline even"><a href="/destinations">Destinations</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline odd"><a href="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/arequipa">Arequipa</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline even last">Arequipa and the Colca Canyon</span></div>												<h1 class="title">Arequipa and the Colca Canyon</h1>
												<div class="tabs"></div>
						<div id="block-system-main" class="block block-system">

    
  <div class="content">
    <div class="tours-full text-justify">
    <div class="field field-name-field-s field-type-image field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><div id="flexslider-1" class="flexslider optionset-default imagestyle-slider-tour">
  <ul class="slides"><li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/colca_4_0.jpg?itok=qJGw1diK" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/santa_catalina2.jpg?itok=lzkEwXwj" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/arequipa_2_0.jpg?itok=o0sMOWOP" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/colca_2_0.jpg?itok=SiTS20f3" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
</ul></div>
</div></div></div>    <div class="box">
        <div class="row">
            <div class="col-sm-9 description-tour"><div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"><p>You will journey to the village of Yura and the Aguada Blanca y Pampa Cañahuas National Reserve, a natural habitat for alpacas and vicuñas.</p>
</div></div></div>            	 <div class="tour-acordion">
	               <div class="panel-group" id="accordion" role="tablist" aria-multiselectable="true">
		               		<div class="btns-itinerary"> 
        	                 
        	                <h2>Itinerary </h2>
				            	     <div class="content-buttons">
                                   <button type="button" class="btns-tour btn_expand" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion">unfold itinerary</button>
                            	   <button type="button" class="btns-tour btn_collapse" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion" data-target=".collapse.in">fold itinerary</button>  
                            	                         			                                 </div>
                        	</div>
                        	<div class="content-itinerary">
                    													<div class="panel panel-default">
            								<div class="panel-heading" role="tab" id="headingOne">
                								<h4 class="panel-title">
               									<button type="button" class="btn btn_acordion" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion" data-target="#collapse15"><span class="glyphicon glyphicon-triangle-bottom"></span><div class="field field-name-field-title-itinerary field-type-text field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>Day 1: Arrival in Arequipa-City Tour-Santa Catalina Convent</p>
</div></div></div></button>
	            								</h4>
            								</div>
           									<div id="collapse15" class="panel-collapse collapse">
                								<div class="panel-body">
                 									<div class="field field-name-field-description-itinerary field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>You arrive in the city of Arequipa and are transferred to your hotel. In the afternoon, you will tour the famed "White City", stopping by the Santa Catalina Convent, a lovely 16th century city in miniature that mimics the styles of different Spanish cities of that time, the Main Square with its three different entrances, and the Church of the Society of Christ, a supreme example of 17th century Mixed Baroque and Spanish Baroque Churrigueresque art, as is the multicolored frescos of the San Ignacio cupola. Following this, you will visit the traditional districts of Cayma and Yanahuara that boasts a lookout and a lovely church.</p>
</div></div></div>                								</div>
            								</div>
        								</div>
         																	<div class="panel panel-default">
            								<div class="panel-heading" role="tab" id="headingOne">
                								<h4 class="panel-title">
               									<button type="button" class="btn btn_acordion" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion" data-target="#collapse16"><span class="glyphicon glyphicon-triangle-bottom"></span><div class="field field-name-field-title-itinerary field-type-text field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>Day 2: Colca Canyon</p>
</div></div></div></button>
	            								</h4>
            								</div>
           									<div id="collapse16" class="panel-collapse collapse">
                								<div class="panel-body">
                 									<div class="field field-name-field-description-itinerary field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>You will journey to the village of Yura and the Aguada Blanca y Pampa Cañahuas National Reserve, a natural habitat for alpacas and vicuñas. You will pause at Patahuasi to rest and drink some coca tea. Afterwards, the drive continues to the valley's main town, Chivay, where you will have lunch and then be transferred to your hotel.Accomodations for the night in Chivay.</p>
</div></div></div>                								</div>
            								</div>
        								</div>
         																	<div class="panel panel-default">
            								<div class="panel-heading" role="tab" id="headingOne">
                								<h4 class="panel-title">
               									<button type="button" class="btn btn_acordion" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion" data-target="#collapse17"><span class="glyphicon glyphicon-triangle-bottom"></span><div class="field field-name-field-title-itinerary field-type-text field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>Day 3: Cruz del Condor - Return to Arequipa</p>
</div></div></div></button>
	            								</h4>
            								</div>
           									<div id="collapse17" class="panel-collapse collapse">
                								<div class="panel-body">
                 									<div class="field field-name-field-description-itinerary field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>Your day begins very early since you are going to the Cruz del Condor lookout, a site where you have spectacular views of one of the deepest canyons in the world. If the conditions are right, you might actually have the chance to take pictures of the majestic condor, world's largest and most powerful bird. Also depending on the program, you might stop at the town of Yanque, where you will experience some local folklore, and visit the villages of Pinchollo and Maca, whose local architecture decorate the Colca Valley.</p>
</div></div></div>                								</div>
            								</div>
        								</div>
         																	<div class="panel panel-default">
            								<div class="panel-heading" role="tab" id="headingOne">
                								<h4 class="panel-title">
               									<button type="button" class="btn btn_acordion" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion" data-target="#collapse18"><span class="glyphicon glyphicon-triangle-bottom"></span><div class="field field-name-field-title-itinerary field-type-text field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>Day 4: Arequipa - Departure</p>
</div></div></div></button>
	            								</h4>
            								</div>
           									<div id="collapse18" class="panel-collapse collapse">
                								<div class="panel-body">
                 									<div class="field field-name-field-description-itinerary field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>At the scheduled time, you will be transferred to the airport for your flight to your next destination.</p>
</div></div></div>                								</div>
            								</div>
        								</div>
         														</div>
						
    				</div>
				</div>

<div class="content-general">
	<div class="zone-content">
		<div class="container">
			    		<h2 class="element-invisible">You are here</h2><div class="breadcrumb"><span class="inline odd first"><a href="/">Home</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline even"><a href="/destinations">Destinations</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline odd"><a href="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/puno">Puno</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline even last">F/D Puno / Sillustani / Lampa / Puno + Almuerzo</span></div>												<h1 class="title">F/D Puno / Sillustani / Lampa / Puno + Almuerzo</h1>
												<div class="tabs"></div>
						<div id="block-system-main" class="block block-system">

    
  <div class="content">
    <div class="tours-full text-justify">
    <div class="field field-name-field-s field-type-image field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><div id="flexslider-1" class="flexslider optionset-default imagestyle-slider-tour">
  <ul class="slides"><li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/sillustani_3.jpg?itok=BZ1StrQq" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/sillustani_2.jpg?itok=eoT09CUq" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/lampa3.jpg?itok=SluNMR0E" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/sillustani_1.jpg?itok=QzleMNnx" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/sillustani_4.jpg?itok=vklNT6Dy" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
</ul></div>
</div></div></div>    <div class="box">
        <div class="row">
            <div class="col-sm-9 description-tour"><div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"><p>SILLUSTANI was the most important Pre-Inca cemetery in Peru, between 600 and 800 years AD, it started by the Qollas but continued in the Inca Empire. It is located on a peninsula on the Umayo Lagoon, which enjoys a very unique atmosphere of tranquility and peace. more than 4000 people are considered buried in this place, with tunnels in their interiors that are still not valued, the most representative are the funerary towers called CHULLPAS, some of them are more than 12 meters high by 7 in diameter, which are not seen elsewhere. In 1973 a studies team from the University of San Marcos, found 503 pieces of gold that belonged to the ornaments of a lord of the Qollas.</p>
</div></div></div>            	 <div class="tour-acordion">
	               <div class="panel-group" id="accordion" role="tablist" aria-multiselectable="true">
		               		<div class="btns-itinerary"> 
        	                 
        	                <h2>Itinerary </h2>
				            	     <div class="content-buttons">
                                   <button type="button" class="btns-tour btn_expand" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion">unfold itinerary</button>
                            	   <button type="button" class="btns-tour btn_collapse" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion" data-target=".collapse.in">fold itinerary</button>  
                            	                         			                                 </div>
                        	</div>
                        	<div class="content-itinerary">
                    													<div class="panel panel-default">
            								<div class="panel-heading" role="tab" id="headingOne">
                								<h4 class="panel-title">
               									<button type="button" class="btn btn_acordion" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion" data-target="#collapse33"><span class="glyphicon glyphicon-triangle-bottom"></span><div class="field field-name-field-title-itinerary field-type-text field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>F/D PUNO / SILLUSTANI / LAMPA / PUNO + ALMUERZO</p>
</div></div></div></button>
	            								</h4>
            								</div>
           									<div id="collapse33" class="panel-collapse collapse">
                								<div class="panel-body">
                 									<div class="field field-name-field-description-itinerary field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>08.00 We left the hotel towards Sillustani<br>
09.00 We arrived at SILLUSTANI.<br>
SILLUSTANI was the most important Pre-Inca cemetery in Peru, between 600 and 800 years AD, it started by the Qollas but continued in the Inca Empire. It is located on a peninsula on the Umayo Lagoon, which enjoys a very unique atmosphere of tranquility and peace. more than 4000 people are considered buried in this place, with tunnels in their interiors that are still not valued, the most representative are the funerary towers called CHULLPAS, some of them are more than 12 meters high by 7 in diameter, which are not seen elsewhere. In 1973 a studies team from the University of San Marcos, found 503 pieces of gold that belonged to the ornaments of a lord of the Qollas.<br>
We also visit some communities that live around the Chullpas that invite us to enter to their houses to share cooked potatoes with cheese, they show us their products, the way that how they weave and develop their textiles, the interior of their rooms and how they raise their animals.<br>
12.00 We will share a traditional lunch in a family house in the community of Hatuncolla.<br>
13.00 After enjoying the delicious lunch, we will go to Lampa<br>
14.30 Lampa is the most preserved Colonial and Republican city in the altiplano, we visited the SANTIAGO APOSTOL Church that began its construction in 1675 and has the only copy of La Piedad made by Miguel Angel and authorized by the Vatican. It also has some catacombs, ossuaries and an exquisite proposal of baroque art in paintings and altarpieces, etc. We also visited Colonial Casonas and Museums. 16.00 After the guided tour, we will return to Puno<br>
17.30 Arrive to Puno and tranfer to your hotel</p>
</div></div></div>                								</div>
            								</div>
        								</div>
         														</div>
						
    				</div>
				</div>

		<div class="container">
			<div id="block-block-8" class="block block-block">

<div class="content-general">
	<div class="zone-content">
		<div class="container">
			    		<h2 class="element-invisible">You are here</h2><div class="breadcrumb"><span class="inline odd first"><a href="/">Home</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline even"><a href="/destinations">Destinations</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline odd"><a href="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/cusco">Cusco</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline even last">Two Days Exploring Into The Sacred Valley</span></div>												<h1 class="title">Two Days Exploring Into The Sacred Valley</h1>
												<div class="tabs"></div>
						<div id="block-system-main" class="block block-system">

    
  <div class="content">
    <div class="tours-full text-justify">
    <div class="field field-name-field-s field-type-image field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><div id="flexslider-1" class="flexslider optionset-default imagestyle-slider-tour">
  <ul class="slides"><li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/machu_picchu_3_0.jpg?itok=sd57ZJvB" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/ollantaytambo3_0.jpg?itok=-d6zfII4" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/moray2_0.jpg?itok=bznVRmix" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/pisac1_0.jpg?itok=erHYZBnu" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
</ul></div>
</div></div></div>    <div class="box">
        <div class="row">
            <div class="col-sm-9 description-tour"><div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"><p>The Sacred Valley of the Incas will welcome us today. This day we will visit the Ccaccaccollo Community to discover a women’s weaving cooperative where we will see and feed the Andean camelids, such as the llamas and alpacas, and where the women will show us all the stages of the traditional weaving process: hand-spinning the wool, dying the wool using natural dyes, and participating in a weaving demonstration.</p>
</div></div></div>            	 <div class="tour-acordion">
	               <div class="panel-group" id="accordion" role="tablist" aria-multiselectable="true">
		               		<div class="btns-itinerary"> 
        	                 
        	                <h2>Itinerary </h2>
				            	     <div class="content-buttons">
                                   <button type="button" class="btns-tour btn_expand" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion">unfold itinerary</button>
                            	   <button type="button" class="btns-tour btn_collapse" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion" data-target=".collapse.in">fold itinerary</button>  
                            	                         			                                 </div>
                        	</div>
                        	<div class="content-itinerary">
                    													<div class="panel panel-default">
            								<div class="panel-heading" role="tab" id="headingOne">
                								<h4 class="panel-title">
               									<button type="button" class="btn btn_acordion" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion" data-target="#collapse37"><span class="glyphicon glyphicon-triangle-bottom"></span><div class="field field-name-field-title-itinerary field-type-text field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>DAY 1:</p>
</div></div></div></button>
	            								</h4>
            								</div>
           									<div id="collapse37" class="panel-collapse collapse">
                								<div class="panel-body">
                 									<div class="field field-name-field-description-itinerary field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>The Sacred Valley of the Incas will welcome us today. This day we will visit the Ccaccaccollo Community to discover a women’s weaving cooperative where we will see and feed the Andean camelids, such as the llamas and alpacas, and where the women will show us all the stages of the traditional weaving process: hand-spinning the wool, dying the wool using natural dyes, and participating in a weaving demonstration. Ccaccaccollo is a community that still have their traditional and ancestors’ customs, with an original heritage and form where you could have an amazing view of the mountains. We will then continue to the Inca and Colonial Pisac to discover one of the most beautiful archeological sites in the Sacred Valley located at the top of the mountain where you can have an amazing view of the colonial town of Pisac. Then, we will have a walking tour to the Colonial town where we will enjoy a delicious lunch. After visited Pisac, we will head to the impressive Inkariy Museum. Here we will take a guided tour of the museum to learn more about the numerous rooms where cultural representations of pre-Hispanic civilizations of ancient Peru are exhibited. Overnight in the Sacred Valley.</p>
</div></div></div>                								</div>
            								</div>
        								</div>
         																	<div class="panel panel-default">
            								<div class="panel-heading" role="tab" id="headingOne">
                								<h4 class="panel-title">
               									<button type="button" class="btn btn_acordion" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion" data-target="#collapse38"><span class="glyphicon glyphicon-triangle-bottom"></span><div class="field field-name-field-title-itinerary field-type-text field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>DAY 2:</p>
</div></div></div></button>
	            								</h4>
            								</div>
           									<div id="collapse38" class="panel-collapse collapse">
                								<div class="panel-body">
                 									<div class="field field-name-field-description-itinerary field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>Our adventure continues exploring the less visited treasures of the Sacred Valley of the Incas. We will start in Moray where the view is awesome due to the colossal concentric terraces simulating an amphitheater. The purpose of it: to recreate 20 different types of microclimates, a measure that guaranteed the agricultural production of the empire. After that, we will go to Maras, the famous and millenary salt mines from colonial times. The contrast of the white wells and the green valley is awesome and a must for a spectacular snapshot of the Sacred Valley of the Incas. We will enjoy a delicious buffet lunch and in the afternoon, we will visit the archaeological site of Ollantaytambo, where we will be able to learn about the technique with which the Incas worked the stones.<br>
Finishing our adventure, we will board the train to Machupicchu Town (Aguas Calientes).</p>
</div></div></div>                								</div>
            								</div>
        								</div>
         														</div>
						
    				</div>
				</div>
           </div>

<div class="content-general">
	<div class="zone-content">
		<div class="container">
			    		<h2 class="element-invisible">You are here</h2><div class="breadcrumb"><span class="inline odd first"><a href="/">Home</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline even"><a href="/destinations">Destinations</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline odd"><a href="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/cusco">Cusco</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline even last">Andean Baroque and South Valley Route</span></div>												<h1 class="title">Andean Baroque and South Valley Route</h1>
												<div class="tabs"></div>
						<div id="block-system-main" class="block block-system">

    
  <div class="content">
    <div class="tours-full text-justify">
    <div class="field field-name-field-s field-type-image field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><div id="flexslider-1" class="flexslider optionset-default imagestyle-slider-tour">
  <ul class="slides"><li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/urcos_templo.jpg?itok=LjKdy0mn" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/pikillacta2_0.jpg?itok=LoZWLS3X" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/tipon_0.jpg?itok=TgfRXDZL" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/andahuaylillas1_0.jpg?itok=rvcl6Vnk" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
</ul></div>
</div></div></div>    <div class="box">
        <div class="row">
            <div class="col-sm-9 description-tour"><div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"><p>The tour starts at 9:00 in the morning. We will depart to Cusco south and after about an hour we will arrive at the Chapel of the Purified Virgin of Canincunca, located on an old Wari center and next to the lagoon of Urcos.</p>
</div></div></div>            	 <div class="tour-acordion">
	               <div class="panel-group" id="accordion" role="tablist" aria-multiselectable="true">
		               		<div class="btns-itinerary"> 
        	                 
        	                <h2>Itinerary </h2>
				            	     <div class="content-buttons">
                                   <button type="button" class="btns-tour btn_expand" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion">unfold itinerary</button>
                            	   <button type="button" class="btns-tour btn_collapse" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion" data-target=".collapse.in">fold itinerary</button>  
                            	                         			                                 </div>
                        	</div>
                        	<div class="content-itinerary">
                    													<div class="panel panel-default">
            								<div class="panel-heading" role="tab" id="headingOne">
                								<h4 class="panel-title">
               									<button type="button" class="btn btn_acordion" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion" data-target="#collapse43"><span class="glyphicon glyphicon-triangle-bottom"></span><div class="field field-name-field-title-itinerary field-type-text field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>Day 1:</p>
</div></div></div></button>
	            								</h4>
            								</div>
           									<div id="collapse43" class="panel-collapse collapse">
                								<div class="panel-body">
                 									<div class="field field-name-field-description-itinerary field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>The tour starts at 9:00 in the morning. We will depart to Cusco south and after about an hour we will arrive at the Chapel of the Purified Virgin of Canincunca, located on an old Wari center and next to the lagoon of Urcos.</p>
<p>Then just 4 minutes from Canincunca is the San Juan Bautista Temple of Huaro, our second destination, which preserves more than 60 sculptures and 50 canvases of great quality and beauty, as well as silverware, altarpieces and others.</p>
<p>Our third destination will be the Temple of San Pedro Apóstol of Andahuaylillas, whose artistic majesty is also reflected in the coffered ceiling of Mudejar influence, the great variety and richness of the canvases (such as the series dedicated to Saint Peter the Apostle, patron saint of the town), the polychromy of the roofs and the triumphal arch that separates the presbytery from the main nave.</p>
<p>After visiting this Temple, we can enjoy a delicious lunch in Andahuaylillas or a generous box lunch.</p>
<p>After having lunch, we will visit Rumiqolqa, that was an inka gate which is located in the eastern sector of the pre-Hispanic city of Pikillacta, this inka gate was one of the main entries to the city of Cusco and exit towards the Qollasuyo.</p>
<p>To complete this tour, we will visit the most important archaeological center regarding the hydraulic wisdom of the Incas: Tipón, which was a major shrine where water was worshiped with the care and veneration that the Incas treated to this element. This complex has been distinguished by the American Society of Civil Engineers as a marvel of Civil Engineering.</p>
<p>We will be arriving in Cusco around 5:00 in the afternoon, after enjoying the Andean Baroque and the South Valley Route.</p>
</div></div></div>                								</div>
            								</div>
        								</div>
         														</div>

                	Contact                	</a>

			    		<h2 class="element-invisible">You are here</h2><div class="breadcrumb"><span class="inline odd first"><a href="/">Home</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline even"><a href="/destinations">Destinations</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline odd"><a href="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/arequipa">Arequipa</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline even last">Misti Volcano</span></div>												<h1 class="title">Misti Volcano</h1>

  <div class="content">
    <div class="tours-full text-justify">
    <div class="field field-name-field-s field-type-image field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><div id="flexslider-1" class="flexslider optionset-default imagestyle-slider-tour">

            <div class="col-sm-9 description-tour"><div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"><p>View of the enormous crater and a second one smaller characterized for emanation of some gases in the bottom, earth with coloration of sulfurates, walk until the point called the cross of the misti: to 5,825 meters. Impressive view of the city of arequipa, and the snowy chachani, pichu pichu., coropuna and ampato mountains.</p>
</div></div></div>            	 <div class="tour-acordion">
	               <div class="panel-group" id="accordion" role="tablist" aria-multiselectable="true">
		               		<div class="btns-itinerary"> 
        	                 
        	                <h2>Itinerary </h2>
				            	     <div class="content-buttons">
                                   <button type="button" class="btns-tour btn_expand" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion">unfold itinerary</button>
                            	   <button type="button" class="btns-tour btn_collapse" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion" data-target=".collapse.in">fold itinerary</button>  
                            	                         			                                 </div>
                        	</div>
                        	<div class="content-itinerary">
                    													<div class="panel panel-default">
            								<div class="panel-heading" role="tab" id="headingOne">
                								<h4 class="panel-title">
               									<button type="button" class="btn btn_acordion" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion" data-target="#collapse28"><span class="glyphicon glyphicon-triangle-bottom"></span><div class="field field-name-field-title-itinerary field-type-text field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>DAY 1: AREQUIPA / CAMP SITE</p>
</div></div></div></button>
	            								</h4>
            								</div>
           									<div id="collapse28" class="panel-collapse collapse">
                								<div class="panel-body">
                 									<div class="field field-name-field-description-itinerary field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>07:00 leave in private car 4 x 4, cabrerias, national reserve of aguada blanca if possible see wild vicuñas, between the snowy misti and chachani, north base of the misti. To 3,800 meters (car base).<br>
08:30 aprox. Beginning of the trekking up to the 4,800.<br>
13:00 brief stop for lunch and restart of the trekk in east direction, accentuated land in volcanic ash.<br>
16:30 arrival to the camp base. Called mont blanc.<br>
Dinner and spend the night at 4800 meters.</p>
</div></div></div>                								</div>
            								</div>
        								</div>
         																	<div class="panel panel-default">
            								<div class="panel-heading" role="tab" id="headingOne">
                								<h4 class="panel-title">
               									<button type="button" class="btn btn_acordion" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion" data-target="#collapse29"><span class="glyphicon glyphicon-triangle-bottom"></span><div class="field field-name-field-title-itinerary field-type-text field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>DAY 2: SUMMIT AND RETURN TO AREQUIPA</p>
</div></div></div></button>
	            								</h4>
            								</div>
           									<div id="collapse29" class="panel-collapse collapse">
                								<div class="panel-body">
                 									<div class="field field-name-field-description-itinerary field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>03:00 breakfast and beginning of the climbing with light equipment trekking of 3 hours, brief rest at: 5,600 meters. Then attack to the summit.<br>
08:00 summit, view of the enormous crater and a second one smaller characterized for emanation of some gases in the bottom, earth with coloration of sulfurates, walk until the point called the cross of the misti: to 5,825 meters. Impressive view of the city of arequipa, and the snowy chachani, pichu pichu., coropuna and ampato mountains.<br>
10:00 beginning of the descent until camp base, rest, walk down to car base and return to arequipa. 16:30 approx in arequipa.</p>
</div></div></div>                								</div>
            								</div>
        								</div>

	<div class="zone-content">
		<div class="container">
			    		<h2 class="element-invisible">You are here</h2><div class="breadcrumb"><span class="inline odd first"><a href="/">Home</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline even"><a href="/destinations">Destinations</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline odd"><a href="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/puno">Puno</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline even last">F/D Kayaking Puno / Uros / Llachon / Taquile</span></div>												<h1 class="title">F/D Kayaking Puno / Uros / Llachon / Taquile</h1>
												<div class="tabs"></div>
						<div id="block-system-main" class="block block-system">

    
  <div class="content">
    <div class="tours-full text-justify">
    <div class="field field-name-field-s field-type-image field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><div id="flexslider-1" class="flexslider optionset-default imagestyle-slider-tour">
  <ul class="slides"><li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/kayaking_puno_1.jpg?itok=qu6dWQw4" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/kayaking_puno_2.jpg?itok=cUP1um2C" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/kayaking_puno_3.jpg?itok=mK2smWeG" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
</ul></div>
</div></div></div>    <div class="box">
        <div class="row">
            <div class="col-sm-9 description-tour"><div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"><p>Transfer from your hotel to the Esteves Island's bay where the guide will gives you a brief talk about the adventure, then begins the route of the Kayak paddling for 1 hour and 30 minutes. We go into the totorales of the National Reserve of Titicaca, where we find indescribable landscapes, the flora and fauna of Titicaca and inhabitants with their daily customs framed by the mountains that surround the lake.</p>
</div></div></div>            	 <div class="tour-acordion">
	               <div class="panel-group" id="accordion" role="tablist" aria-multiselectable="true">
		               		<div class="btns-itinerary"> 
        	                 
        	                <h2>Itinerary </h2>
				            	     <div class="content-buttons">
                                   <button type="button" class="btns-tour btn_expand" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion">unfold itinerary</button>
                            	   <button type="button" class="btns-tour btn_collapse" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion" data-target=".collapse.in">fold itinerary</button>  
                            	                         			                                 </div>
                        	</div>
                        	<div class="content-itinerary">
                    													<div class="panel panel-default">
            								<div class="panel-heading" role="tab" id="headingOne">
                								<h4 class="panel-title">
               									<button type="button" class="btn btn_acordion" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion" data-target="#collapse32"><span class="glyphicon glyphicon-triangle-bottom"></span><div class="field field-name-field-title-itinerary field-type-text field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>F/D KAYAKING PUNO / UROS / LLACHON / TAQUILE</p>
</div></div></div></button>
	            								</h4>
            								</div>
           									<div id="collapse32" class="panel-collapse collapse">
                								<div class="panel-body">
                 									<div class="field field-name-field-description-itinerary field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>06.45: Transfer from your hotel to the Esteves Island's bay where the guide will gives you a brief talk about the adventure, then begins the route of the Kayak paddling for 1 hour and 30 minutes. We go into the totorales of the National Reserve of Titicaca, where we find indescribable landscapes, the flora and fauna of Titicaca and inhabitants with their daily customs framed by the mountains that surround the lake. We will visit the Devil's Island and arriving at the Uros, the guide will begin with the explanation of the floating islands, then you will have free time to explore the island, visit family houses, photoshoot. Finishing the whole journey, we will continue traveling by motor boat to the Llachón Peninsula (1hour and 30min.), and then we will continue paddling to Taquile island (1 hour and 30min.), on route you can see: the crystal clear waters of Titikaka, the Amantani and Taquile Islands and the Real Cordillera of Bolivia. Reaching Taquile, you can see the life way of their inhabitants, their customs and traditions, the traditional costumes and crafs of the place. We will enjoy a delicious lunch made by the locals and after visited de place, we will return to Puno by motor boat, arriving at 5:00 p.m.</p>
</div></div></div>                								</div>
            								</div>
        								</div>
         														</div>
						
    				</div>
				</div>

			    		<h2 class="element-invisible">You are here</h2><div class="breadcrumb"><span class="inline odd first"><a href="/">Home</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline even"><a href="/destinations">Destinations</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline odd"><a href="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/cusco">Cusco</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline even last">Two Days Experienced-Based Tourism in Mullakas Misminay</span></div>												<h1 class="title">Two Days Experienced-Based Tourism in Mullakas Misminay</h1>

    <div class="tours-full text-justify">
    <div class="field field-name-field-s field-type-image field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><div id="flexslider-1" class="flexslider optionset-default imagestyle-slider-tour">
  <ul class="slides"><li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/mullakas_misminay_3.jpg?itok=bV3YSzpm" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/mullakas_misminay_1.jpg?itok=qDNqMG-C" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/mullakas_misminay_2.jpg?itok=LZWkwVBo" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/mullakas_misminay_4.jpg?itok=dEvKM5hW" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
</ul></div>
</div></div></div>    <div class="box">
        <div class="row">
            <div class="col-sm-9 description-tour"><div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"><p>The Experienced-Based Tourism in Mullakas Misminay, will take you to know the parts of the Sacred Valley, a journey full of living culture and customs that were not lost with the passage of time. It will allow us to directly enter in contact with the whole community and be close to the way of life of the people, eat with them, work, share their beliefs, cook, and participate in all their daily activities. In this way, both parties, you and the people, learn the different cultures, one from the other. More than anything, it is learning from shared and lived experience.</p>
<p>The Community of Mullakas Misminay is located near the District of Maras, which has great landscapes and colorful fields of culture.</p>
<p>Over time, they were in charge of producing beautiful colored fabrics, with Andean designs, a heritage that they received from many past generations. Enjoy a wonderful and charming stay in the Sacred Valley, rest assured that it will have the best service and you will feel like the millenary culture captures you in its magic of the Andes.</p>
</div></div></div>            	 <div class="tour-acordion">
	               <div class="panel-group" id="accordion" role="tablist" aria-multiselectable="true">
		               		<div class="btns-itinerary"> 
        	                 
        	                <h2>Itinerary </h2>
				            	     <div class="content-buttons">
                                   <button type="button" class="btns-tour btn_expand" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion">unfold itinerary</button>
                            	   <button type="button" class="btns-tour btn_collapse" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion" data-target=".collapse.in">fold itinerary</button>  
                            	                         			                                 </div>
                        	</div>
                        	<div class="content-itinerary">
                    													<div class="panel panel-default">
            								<div class="panel-heading" role="tab" id="headingOne">
                								<h4 class="panel-title">
               									<button type="button" class="btn btn_acordion" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion" data-target="#collapse39"><span class="glyphicon glyphicon-triangle-bottom"></span><div class="field field-name-field-title-itinerary field-type-text field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>Day 1: Cusco – Maras – Moray</p>
</div></div></div></button>
	            								</h4>
            								</div>
           									<div id="collapse39" class="panel-collapse collapse">
                								<div class="panel-body">
                 									<div class="field field-name-field-description-itinerary field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>The first day of the tour, we will pick you up at 07:00 in the morning from your hotel to take you to Maras, on route we will appreciate the diverse and impressive places that the Sacred Valley lodges. We will make a brief stop at the Raqchi viewpoint to be able to see the imposing snow- capped mountains of Chicon, Salkantay and Veronica.</p>
<p>Then, we will arrive to the village of Maras to continue on route to the Salineras, where we can contemplate its 3,000 wells of salt that were used in the Incas food until our days. Later, we will go to the circular farming terraces of Moray.</p>
<p>In this way, we will reach the community of Misminay where they will receive us in the middle of music and dance to take us to the small houses; they will be waiting for us with a delicious lunch. Finished the meal, they will guide us towards the viewpoint of the Waninmarca mountain, from here we will obtain fabulous views of Moray and the Sacred Valley. Arrival at night, we will have a family dinner with a nocturnal fire full of stories and traditional legends.</p>
</div></div></div>                								</div>
            								</div>
        								</div>
         																	<div class="panel panel-default">
            								<div class="panel-heading" role="tab" id="headingOne">
                								<h4 class="panel-title">
               									<button type="button" class="btn btn_acordion" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion" data-target="#collapse40"><span class="glyphicon glyphicon-triangle-bottom"></span><div class="field field-name-field-title-itinerary field-type-text field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>Day 2: Agriculture – Textile Weaving – Cusco</p>
</div></div></div></button>
	            								</h4>
            								</div>
           									<div id="collapse40" class="panel-collapse collapse">
                								<div class="panel-body">
                 									<div class="field field-name-field-description-itinerary field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>We will wake up early to enjoy a nutritious breakfast with products and Andean cereals of the area and thus direct ourselves to carry out agricultural activities such as plowing or harvesting in the fields, but before this a payment will be made to the Pachamama and the Apus in gratitude for the food that give us. Later, we will learn a little about the elaboration of the textile garments with the ancestral techniques and with the use of natural products that the nature gives us. Later we be able to cook a delicious lunch based on products of the area, we will participate in the elaboration of the Pachamanca, a delicious and representative dish of the Andean region. After delighting us with the exquisite dish prepared by the residents and carrying out the daily activities, in the afternoon we will be back to the city of Cusco and return to our hotel.</p>
<p>*This day we can chose the activities to do in the community, we have many options. Maximum altitude: 3,700 meters / 12,139 feet.</p>
</div></div></div>                								</div>
            								</div>
        								</div>
         														</div>

    if (advagg_mod_1.count <= 40) {

      // Set this to 100 so that this function only runs once.
      advagg_mod_1.count = 100;
    }
  }
  catch(e) {
    if (advagg_mod_1.count >= 40) {
      // Throw the exception if this still fails after running 40 times.
      throw e;

function advagg_mod_1_check() {
  if (window.jQuery && window.Drupal && window.Drupal.settings) {
    advagg_mod_1();

  }

<div class="content-general">
	<div class="zone-content">
		<div class="container">
			    		<h2 class="element-invisible">You are here</h2><div class="breadcrumb"><span class="inline odd first"><a href="/">Home</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline even"><a href="/destinations">Destinations</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline odd"><a href="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/cusco">Cusco</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline even last">Inca Trail Express</span></div>												<h1 class="title">Inca Trail Express</h1>
												<div class="tabs"></div>
						<div id="block-system-main" class="block block-system">

    
  <div class="content">
    <div class="tours-full text-justify">
    <div class="field field-name-field-s field-type-image field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><div id="flexslider-1" class="flexslider optionset-default imagestyle-slider-tour">
  <ul class="slides"><li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/incatrail1.jpg?itok=wiU88Lpc" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/incatrail2.jpg?itok=Z3okXCLk" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/incatrail3.jpg?itok=a6sbjr5u" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/incatrail4.jpg?itok=eji5J9Ji" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/machu_picchu4.jpg?itok=sivgtZUW" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
</ul></div>
</div></div></div>    <div class="box">
        <div class="row">
            <div class="col-sm-9 description-tour"><div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"><p>Inca Trail Express is a one-day trek along the final well-preserved stretch of the classic trail to Machu Picchu. Start at KM104 for Chachabamba ruins before ascending to Wiñay Wayna, which means ‘forever young’ in Quechua. Continue towards Intipunku, the Sun Gate, for your first glimpse of the ancient citadel of Machu Picchu. Descend along the trail, admiring the views as get closer to the ruins.</p>
<p>The next day we return to Machu Picchu for a guided tour to learn about the different sectors of this ancient city whilst learning about Inca history.</p>
</div></div></div>            	 <div class="tour-acordion">
	               <div class="panel-group" id="accordion" role="tablist" aria-multiselectable="true">
		               		<div class="btns-itinerary"> 
        	                 
        	                <h2>Itinerary </h2>
				            	     <div class="content-buttons">
                                   <button type="button" class="btns-tour btn_expand" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion">unfold itinerary</button>
                            	   <button type="button" class="btns-tour btn_collapse" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion" data-target=".collapse.in">fold itinerary</button>  
                            	                         			                                 </div>
                        	</div>
                        	<div class="content-itinerary">
                    													<div class="panel panel-default">
            								<div class="panel-heading" role="tab" id="headingOne">
                								<h4 class="panel-title">
               									<button type="button" class="btn btn_acordion" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion" data-target="#collapse41"><span class="glyphicon glyphicon-triangle-bottom"></span><div class="field field-name-field-title-itinerary field-type-text field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>Day 1 CUSCO / KM. 104 / CHACHABAMBA / WIÑAY WAYNA / MACHU PICCHU</p>
</div></div></div></button>
	            								</h4>
            								</div>
           									<div id="collapse41" class="panel-collapse collapse">
                								<div class="panel-body">
                 									<div class="field field-name-field-description-itinerary field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>Transfer to the train station at Ollantaytambo for an early departure to KM104, the start of the Inca Trail Express. We will cross the hanging bridge to the Chachabamba site and after a brief visit we begin the 3-hour ascent to the ruins of Wiñay Wayna, an important spiritual site. The Inca Trail cuts across the ridge above Machu Picchu to finally reach Intipunku (the Sun Gate) from where we will have an amazing first view of Machupicchu and where the trail winds downhill.<br>
This day we will have a box lunch on route.</p>
<p>The classic vista from the Sun Gate to the citadel is a truly unique experience, an unforgettable way for your first view of this magical site. After arriving to Machupicchu, we will descend by bus to Machupicchu Town (Aguas Calientes) and overnight at your chosen hotel with dinner included. (B/BL/D)</p>
</div></div></div>                								</div>
            								</div>
        								</div>
         																	<div class="panel panel-default">
            								<div class="panel-heading" role="tab" id="headingOne">
                								<h4 class="panel-title">
               									<button type="button" class="btn btn_acordion" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion" data-target="#collapse42"><span class="glyphicon glyphicon-triangle-bottom"></span><div class="field field-name-field-title-itinerary field-type-text field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>Day 2 MACHU PICCHU / CUSCO</p>
</div></div></div></button>
	            								</h4>
            								</div>
           									<div id="collapse42" class="panel-collapse collapse">
                								<div class="panel-body">
                 									<div class="field field-name-field-description-itinerary field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>Early departure from your hotel for your guided visit of Machu Picchu which takes around 3 hours. Walking through the different sectors of the hill-top citadel and learning about different aspects of Inca life and history as you admire the mist cloaked mountains.</p>
<p>After our visit to this beautiful Citadel, we will return to Aguas Calientes for lunch before boarding the train to Ollantaytambo or Poroy and then transfer to your hotel. (B/L)</p>
<p><strong>*This day and depend of the availability, we will have the option to visit Huaynapicchu or Machupicchu Mountain.</strong></p>
</div></div></div>                								</div>
            								</div>
        								</div>
         														</div>
						
    				</div>
				</div>
           </div>

                       <div class="field field-name-field-recommendations field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p><strong>What to take:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Comfortable walking shoes</li>
<li>Standard clothing used for travelling outdoor worldwide</li>
<li>Outdoor gear including rain protection</li>
<li>Sunscreen and insect repellent</li>
<li>Warm clothes especially in the months of May – July when temperatures can vary from hot days to freezing nights.</li>
</ul>
<p>Personal first aid kit. On each trip we carry a medical kit but we suggest a small personal first- aid kit for bruises and blisters. A knee and ankle brace are sometimes useful especially if you suffer from weak knees or ankles. Include any special medication your doctor might suggest for you.</p>

		<div class="container">
			    		<h2 class="element-invisible">You are here</h2><div class="breadcrumb"><span class="inline odd first"><a href="/">Home</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline even"><a href="/destinations">Destinations</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline odd"><a href="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/lima">Lima</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline even last">Colonial &amp; Modern Lima City Tour</span></div>												<h1 class="title">Colonial &amp; Modern Lima City Tour</h1>
												<div class="tabs"></div>
						<div id="block-system-main" class="block block-system">

    
  <div class="content">
    <div class="tours-full text-justify">
    <div class="field field-name-field-s field-type-image field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><div id="flexslider-1" class="flexslider optionset-default imagestyle-slider-tour">
  <ul class="slides"><li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/lima-colonial-y-moderna-slider-1.jpg?itok=wmDNNKcs" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/lima-colonial-y-moderna-slider-2.jpg?itok=DSVd34j8" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/lima-colonial-y-moderna-slider-3.jpg?itok=tax6SZDF" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/lima-colonial-y-moderna-slider-4.jpg?itok=OvsYBxJ8" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
</ul></div>
</div></div></div>    <div class="box">
        <div class="row">
            <div class="col-sm-9 description-tour"><div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"><p>A tour of the best of colonial and modern Lima, including the most imposing colonial churches and mansions such as the Government Palace, Plaza Mayor, the City and the Cathedral and the Convento de San Francisco, jewels of the sixteenth century colonial architecture. On our way to southern and modern Lima City, we will stop by the Larco Museum, which is located in an impressive 18th century colonial mansion built over a 7th century pyramid. The museum overlooks a colourful garden that won the prize for the best garden in Lima in 2009 in its category. It has recently been renovated and displays a remarkable collection of pre-Columbian art including crowns, earrings, nose ornaments, garments, masks and vases, and jewelry finely wrought in gold and decorated with semi-precious stones. In the erotic gallery you will be intrigued by all the Moche ithyphallic jars and by the ceramic pots showing, in a very certainly realistic and humoristic way, their sexual habits. The Larco Museum is also one of the few museums in the world that allows tourists to go into the storage area. In total, there are more than 45,000 pieces to enjoy, making the Larco Museum an unforgettable and unique experience. We will enjoy lunch in the Museum’s Restaurant, which offers a varied and select house menu, which showcases the flavors, products and customs of our country, giving it a character, which reflects the vibrancy of modern Peru. Later the tour continues to the modern district of San Isidro, where we will visit the Huaca Huallamarca, an adobe pre-Inca pyramid, and then we will end at Miraflores, walking in the Love Park with splendid views of the Pacific Ocean.</p>
</div></div></div>            	 <div class="tour-acordion">
