	<div class="zone-content">
		<div class="container">
			    		<h2 class="element-invisible">You are here</h2><div class="breadcrumb"><span class="inline odd first"><a href="/">Home</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline even"><a href="/destinations">Destinations</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline odd"><a href="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/arequipa">Arequipa</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline even last">Arequipa Basic</span></div>												<h1 class="title">Arequipa Basic</h1>
												<div class="tabs"></div>
						<div id="block-system-main" class="block block-system">

    
  <div class="content">
    <div class="tours-full text-justify">
    <div class="field field-name-field-s field-type-image field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><div id="flexslider-1" class="flexslider optionset-default imagestyle-slider-tour">
  <ul class="slides"><li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/arequipa_1.jpg?itok=51OWxQLk" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/arequipa_2.jpg?itok=F60TYWyG" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/santa_catalina.jpg?itok=Vhc_fVLP" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/yahanhuara.jpg?itok=iSP9xrve" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
</ul></div>
</div></div></div>    <div class="box">
        <div class="row">
            <div class="col-sm-9 description-tour"><div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"><p>You arrive in the city of Arequipa and are transferred to your hotel. In the afternoon, you will tour the famed "White City", stopping by the Santa Catalina Convent, a lovely 16th century city in miniature that mimics the styles of different Spanish cities of that time, the Main Square with its three different entrances, and the Church of the Society of Christ, a supreme example of 17th century Mixed Baroque and Spanish Baroque Churrigueresque art, as is the multicolored frescos of the San Ignacio cupola.</p>
</div></div></div>            	 <div class="tour-acordion">
	               <div class="panel-group" id="accordion" role="tablist" aria-multiselectable="true">
		               		<div class="btns-itinerary"> 
        	                 
        	                <h2>Itinerary </h2>
				            	     <div class="content-buttons">
                                   <button type="button" class="btns-tour btn_expand" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion">unfold itinerary</button>

               									<button type="button" class="btn btn_acordion" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion" data-target="#collapse19"><span class="glyphicon glyphicon-triangle-bottom"></span><div class="field field-name-field-title-itinerary field-type-text field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>Day 1: Arrival in Arequipa-City Tour-Santa Catalina Convent</p>
</div></div></div></button>
	            								</h4>
            								</div>
           									<div id="collapse19" class="panel-collapse collapse">
                								<div class="panel-body">
                 									<div class="field field-name-field-description-itinerary field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>You arrive in the city of Arequipa and are transferred to your hotel. In the afternoon, you will tour the famed "White City", stopping by the Santa Catalina Convent, a lovely 16th century city in miniature that mimics the styles of different Spanish cities of that time, the Main Square with its three different entrances, and the Church of the Society of Christ, a supreme example of 17th century Mixed Baroque and Spanish Baroque Churrigueresque art, as is the multicolored frescos of the San Ignacio cupola. Following this, you will visit the traditional districts of Cayma and Yanahuara that boasts a lookout and a lovely church.</p>
</div></div></div>                								</div>
            								</div>

</div></div></div></button>
	            								</h4>

The Founder’s Mansion and impressive Terraces. Enjoy a traditional lunch in a local restaurant</p>

		<div class="container">
			    		<h2 class="element-invisible">You are here</h2><div class="breadcrumb"><span class="inline odd first"><a href="/">Home</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline even"><a href="/destinations">Destinations</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline odd"><a href="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/puno">Puno</a></span> <span class="delimiter">&gt;</span> <span class="inline even last">2D / 1N Uros + Ovenight in Amantani + Taquile, PVT (private)</span></div>												<h1 class="title">2D / 1N Uros + Ovenight in Amantani + Taquile, PVT (private)</h1>
												<div class="tabs"></div>
						<div id="block-system-main" class="block block-system">

    
  <div class="content">
    <div class="tours-full text-justify">
    <div class="field field-name-field-s field-type-image field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><div id="flexslider-1" class="flexslider optionset-default imagestyle-slider-tour">
  <ul class="slides"><li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/amantani_3.jpg?itok=FSbt4-IU" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/uros_1_0.jpg?itok=sIES3MQm" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/taquile1_0.jpg?itok=p9OfVSWA" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/amantani_1.jpg?itok=S0l6SqVS" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
<li><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.justenjoyperu.com/files/styles/slider_tour/public/amantani_2.jpg?itok=kW7mvvM2" width="1170" height="500" alt="" title=""></li>
</ul></div>
</div></div></div>    <div class="box">
        <div class="row">
            <div class="col-sm-9 description-tour"><div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"><p>Arrival in Taquile, we enter into paths with agricultural lands, surprising landscapes among the colors of the costumes, the immense lake and as a backdrop, the snow- caped mountains of Illimani. We arrive at the town to have a representation of handicrafts, after that, we will visit the touristic interest places. Taquile has been recognized by UNESCO as a World Heritage Site for the textiles they present, with iconographies representing their customs, calendars, etc.</p>
</div></div></div>            	 <div class="tour-acordion">
	               <div class="panel-group" id="accordion" role="tablist" aria-multiselectable="true">
		               		<div class="btns-itinerary"> 
        	                 
        	                <h2>Itinerary </h2>
				            	     <div class="content-buttons">
                                   <button type="button" class="btns-tour btn_expand" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion">unfold itinerary</button>
                            	   <button type="button" class="btns-tour btn_collapse" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion" data-target=".collapse.in">fold itinerary</button>  
                            	                         			                                 </div>
                        	</div>
                        	<div class="content-itinerary">
                    													<div class="panel panel-default">
            								<div class="panel-heading" role="tab" id="headingOne">
                								<h4 class="panel-title">
               									<button type="button" class="btn btn_acordion" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion" data-target="#collapse30"><span class="glyphicon glyphicon-triangle-bottom"></span><div class="field field-name-field-title-itinerary field-type-text field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>DAY 01: UROS + OVERNIGHT IN AMANTANI</p>
</div></div></div></button>
	            								</h4>
            								</div>
           									<div id="collapse30" class="panel-collapse collapse">
                								<div class="panel-body">
                 									<div class="field field-name-field-description-itinerary field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>08:00 Transfer from your Hotel to the Port of Puno with a private guide and transportation<br>
08:40 Visit to the Floating Islands of the Uros, the ethnic group that arrived in Puno 3700 years ago according to the National Geographic and that survived thanks to its ability to live among the cattails until today with customs of collectors and fishermen. In a hundred of islands, approximately two thousand people live.<br>
09:50 Departure to Amantani<br>
12:50 Arrival in Amantani. We enter in paths full of vegetation, accompanied by locals with colorful costumes that greet us until we reach their warm beautifull houses that will host us. Amantani is the most energetic island on the lake, many mystical groups visit it because has two important ceremonial centers, the PACHA TATA and PACHA MAMA mountains that has millenary constructions for rituals that are performed only once a year due to its importance<br>
13:20 Lunch<br>
15:00 Ascent to Pacha Tata at more than 4,100 high, it is the main mystic ceremonial center of Titicaca, until waiting for the indescribable sunset in the immensity of Titicaca. 19:00 Dinner<br>
20:00 The locals share their traditional costumes with all the visitors that want to try them to attend a community meeting or to a mystical sessions.</p>
</div></div></div>                								</div>
            								</div>
        								</div>
         																	<div class="panel panel-default">
            								<div class="panel-heading" role="tab" id="headingOne">
                								<h4 class="panel-title">
               									<button type="button" class="btn btn_acordion" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion" data-target="#collapse31"><span class="glyphicon glyphicon-triangle-bottom"></span><div class="field field-name-field-title-itinerary field-type-text field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>DAY 02: TAQUILE ISLAND AND RETURN TO PUNO</p>
</div></div></div></button>
	            								</h4>
            								</div>
           									<div id="collapse31" class="panel-collapse collapse">
                								<div class="panel-body">
                 									<div class="field field-name-field-description-itinerary field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><p>
07:30 Breakfast<br>
08:00 We embarked to travel to the Taquile island.<br>
09:00 Arrival in Taquile, we enter into paths with agricultural lands, surprising landscapes among the colors of the costumes, the immense lake and as a backdrop, the snow- caped mountains of Illimani. We arrive at the town to have a representation of handicrafts, after that, we will visit the touristic interest places. Taquile has been recognized by UNESCO as a World Heritage Site for the textiles they present, with iconographies representing their customs, calendars, etc.<br>
12:00 Lunch accompanied by dances and music, photo session with traditional costumes. Return to the Port of Puno<br>
16:00 Arrival at the Port. Transfer to your respective Hotel</p>
</div></div></div>                								</div>
            								</div>
        								</div>
         														</div>
						
    				</div>
				</div>
           </div>
